Name:TP.TPCHIP.NET.PCBMS.QRESET_REG
Constant(s):
Comments:
SelectedAttributes:
LatchesBitsLatch Name [flushval]
Bit(s)SCOM Dial: Description
0 WO_1P qreset_pcb
Write access to this register will lead to trigger of auto sequencing of quiesce and reset

Ignore parity register. If set to 1, accesses to the PCB master get forwarded to PCB, also all interrupts are forwarded to the interrupt controller. If set to 0, accesses with parity error to the PCB master do not get forwarded to the PCB, interrupt packets with parity error do not get forwarded to the interrupt controller.
Addr: 00000000000F001C (SCOM)
Name:TP.TPCHIP.NET.PCBMS.IGNORE_PAR_REG
Constant(s):
Comments:
SelectedAttributes:
LatchesBitsLatch Name [flushval]
0:4TP.TPCHIP.NET.PCBMS.COMP.PCBMS_REGFILE.IGNORE_PAR_REG_LT_INST.LATC.L2(0:4) [00000]
Bit(s)SCOM Dial: Description
0 RW IGNORE_PARITY_REG: Set to 0 to block accesses with parity errors from PCB, also to ignore interrupt packets with parity error.
1 RW DISABLE_ECC_CORRECTION: If set, the ECC error correction feature is off.
2 RWX_WCLRPART ECC_S_BIT_ERROR: Set by HW on single-bit ECC error. Cleared on writing
3 RW ENABLE_BNDY_LATS: If set, boundary latches are enabled
4 RW ENABLE_EXTENDED_RSP: If set, extended error response is put on rsp_data

3 RW CFG_DISABLE_CL_ATOMIC_LOCK: Disable atomic lock for chiplet accesses
4 RW CFG_DISABLE_HEARTBEAT: Disable check for voltage and gridclock in the chiplet

10 RW CFG_MASK_HEARTBEAT_ERRS: Mask missing heartbeat errors (error register bit 17)

12:19 RW CFG_MASK_PLL_ERRS: Mask PLL unlock errors (error register bits 24:31)

21 RW CFG_FORCE_0_QME: Disable, force-to-zero in QME Master Interface Response Data on non-zero response info.
22 RW MASK_QME_RISING_EDGE_DETECTED_ON_QUIESCE: Mask FIR propogation - QME rising edge detected

Bit(s)SCOM Dial: Description
0 RWX_WCLEAR CE_ERROR: Correctable error on PCb Network
1:3 RWX_WCLEAR CHIPLET_ERRORS: Errors reported from End-points/Chiplet, including QME Slave End-point 000 = no error 001 = XSCOM command blocked due pending errors 010 = chiplet offline 011 = partial good 100 = invalid address / address error / bad access type 101 = clock error 110 = parity error / received unexpected packet / wrong packet number 111 = timeout This register is for debug purposes only. It only holds meaningful data if it is cleared after each error. These bits can be set when a transaction is initiated by both PCB Master as well as QME Master
4 RWX_WCLEAR PARITY_ERROR: Parity error/ECC Error on PCB Network
5 RWX_WCLEAR DATA_BUFFER_ERROR: Parity error in PCB Master Request Data
6 RWX_WCLEAR ADDR_BUFFER_ERROR: Parity error in PCB Master Request address
7 RWX_WCLEAR PCB_FSM_ERROR: Invalid state error in PCB FSM
8 RWX_WCLEAR CL_FSM_ERROR: Invalid state error in Chiplet FSM These bits can be set when a transaction is initiated by both PCB Master as well as QME Master
9 RWX_WCLEAR INT_RX_FSM_ERROR: Invalid state error in interrupt RX FSM
10 RWX_WCLEAR INT_TX_FSM_ERROR: Invalid state error in interrupt TX FSM
11 RWX_WCLEAR INT_TYPE_ERROR: Invalid interrupt type
12 RWX_WCLEAR CL_DATA_ERROR: Parity error on End-point/Chiplet Interface, including QME Slave End-point This bit can be set when a transaction is initiated by both PCB Master as well as QME Master
13 RWX_WCLEAR INFO_ERROR: Parity error on Response Info lines from End-point/Chiplet, including QME Slave End-point This bit can be set when a transaction is initiated by both PCB Master as well as QME Master
14 RWX_WCLEAR SEQ_ERROR: Sequence Error: PCB Slave detected beats sequenced Incorrectly
15 RWX_WCLEAR CHIPLET_ATOMIC_LOCK_ERROR: Atomic lock error in PCB Slave Internal End-point. This bit can be set when a transaction is initiated by both PCB Master as well as QME Master
16 RWX_WCLEAR PCB_INTERFACE_ERROR: Error of pcb interface component for the internal endpoint
17 RWX_WCLEAR CHIPLET_OFFLINE: Heartbeat check indicated that chiplet is offline
18 RWX_WCLEAR EDRAM_SEQUENCE_ERR: Error in edram power up sequence
19 RWX_WCLEAR CTRL_REG_PARITY_ERROR: cntl register parity bad
20 RWX_WCLEAR ADDRESS_REG_PARITY_ERROR: Multicast Group Address register parity bad
21 RWX_WCLEAR TIMEOUT_REG_PARITY_ERROR: Timeout select register parity bad
22 RWX_WCLEAR CONFIG_REG_PARITY_ERROR: Slave config register parity bad
23 RWX_WCLEAR DIV_REG_PARITY_ERROR: Hang Pulse Pre-counter register parity bad

2 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR CLK_ASYNC_RESET: P9 cache chiplet: EQ Skew adjust reset, P9 core chiplet: core duty cycle adjust reset, P9 mem chiplet: mem glsmux async reset
3 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR PLL_TEST_EN: Test enable for chiplet pll
4 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR PLL_RESET: Reset for chiplet pll
5 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR PLL_BYPASS: Enable bypass for chiplet pll
6 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR VITAL_SCAN: Scan control for chiplet vital domain
7 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR VITAL_SCAN_IN: Scan in for the chiplet vital domain
8 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR VITAL_PHASE: Phase for vital domain
9 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR FLUSH_ALIGN_OVR: Override flush, flush_nto1, align in chiplet to 1
10 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR VITAL_AL: Align for vital domain
11 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR ACT_DIS: LCB control signal for vital logic
12 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR TOADMODE_EN: Toad Mode Enable
13 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR SYNC_PULSE: PCB Sync Pulse Disable
14 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR MPW3: Vital Region Clock Gate Disable
15 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR DELAY_LCLKR: LCB control signal for vital logic
16 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR VITAL_THOLD: Thold for the chiplet vital domain
17 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR FLUSH_SCAN_N: Flush scan N
18 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR FENCE_EN: Fencing signal for chiplet
19 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR CPLT_RCTRL: Chiplet receiver enable
20 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR CPLT_DCTRL: Chiplet driver enable
21 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR CPLT_RCTRL2: Chiplet receiver enable 2
22 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR ADJ_FUNC_CLKSEL: P9 chache chiplet: clock select for skew adjust/duty cycle adjust logic, P9 core chiplet: skew sense to skew adjust fencing
23 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR pm_access
24 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR FUNC_LCB_EDIS: Chiplet Func clocks' LCB Test EDIS
25 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR TP_FENCE_PCB: Fence the Chiplet from the PCB Bus. If set, PCB Slave will report 'Chiplet Offline'
26 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR LVLTRANS_FENCE: Unused
27 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR ARRAY_WRITE_ASSIST_EN: Array write assist
28 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR HTB_INTEST: HTB intest mode
29 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR HTB_EXTEST: HTB extest mode
30 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR OOB_PROTECTION: OOB Protection Control - Set it to '1' to prevent OOB from propogating to EPS/QME. Reset signals [*_oob(2) and *_oob_lt(0)] dont get OOB protection
31 RWX RWX_WAND RWX_WOR PLLFORCE_OUT_EN: PLL force out enable
